 khichdi ko bharat ke superfood ke taur par pesh kiye jane ko lekar charchaa bhi khub ho rahi he

 acharya ke mutabik yah khushi kii baat he ki der se hi sahi lekin khichdi ko uskaa sammaan milane ja rahaa he
 Acharya says that khichdi truly represents India because it shows 'unity in diversity' like our country
 khichdi kisi na kisi rup main bharat ke har rajya main khai jaati he, lekin har jagah uskaa swaad uskaa rang rup or usko banane kaa tarika alag alag hota he
 The biggest feature of Khichdi is that it can be changed according to your choice
 khichdi banane ke tareeke main tamaam badlaav karne ke baad bhi iske buniyadi gun or swaad donon bane rahete he
 According to Acharya Bal Krishna, according to Ayurveda, khichdi is considered a very good diet
 yah pachaane main aasaan hoti he

 shishu bhi jab ann khaanaa shuru karte hai to khichdi hi unke munh lagaai jaati he

 ise pakaana bhi bahut aasaan he

 acharya kehete hai ki khichdi ko jo pahchaan or sammaan ab mil rahaa he, wo bahut pehle hi mil janaa chahie tha
 Let us get late, better fit
 depressant se pareshaan log usase mukti paane ke liye kya kuch nahin karte hai

 jarnal of american medical association main prakashit report ke mutabik, nutrishanal supplement aapke depressant ko thik karne main kargar nahin he
 Let me tell you, this study included people from UK, Netherlands, Germany and Spain who are not in depression but are on the verge of having depression
 is study ke liye 1000 logon kaa sample liya gaya he
 In this study, which lasted for one year, some people were given nutritional supplements
 jabaki kuch ko placebo or kuch logon ko lifestil koching di gai
 Although the results of the study are not very positive on any aspect, it has been said that changes in diet and behavioral therapy are capable of reducing depression to some extent
 is study ke shodhakarta professor idi watkin kehete hai, 'depressant ek bahut hi saamaanya samasya ban gai he, jo kaaphi logon ko apni chapet main le rahi he, iskaa samaadhaan nikaalnaa jaruri he

 lekin diet main parivartan karne se depressant main kuch had tak kam ho saktaa he

 rail travelers sarvice agenton (artiese) dwaara tikaton kii ‚Äòbaari‚Äô maatra main booking rail adhikariyon kii mileebhagat se ho rahi he
 a parliamentary committee believes that such illegal activities are going on in connivance with the railway authorities
 loklekha samiti kii report ke masaude main kaha gaya he ki agenton kii is tarah kii avaidh gatividhiyaan bina yatri aarakshan pranali main kaam kar rahe rail adhikariyon kii mileebhagat se nahin ho saktin
 rtsas are licensed agents authorized by the Ministry of Railways to purchase tickets for passengers
 iske liye ve maamuli shulk lete hai
 After examining the immediate and advance reservation system by the PAC, the fact has come to light that the people for whom these schemes are actually not getting the benefit of it, because there is a mess in it
 yah tathy bhi saamne aayaa he ki artiese ke kai aniyamittaaon main shaamil hone ke baavjood pichley 5 saal main unke khilaaf dilli ko chhodkar koi maamla darj nahin hua he
 Nine cases have been filed against him only in Delhi
 samiti ne agenton tathaa rail karmchaariyon ke khilaaf kadi karrwai kii vakaalat karte hue railway se is tarah ke sabhi maamalon kii jaanch karne ko kaha he
 Strict action has been recommended against those involved in such cases
 haalanki artiese kii niyukti railway dwaara kii jaati he, lekin computerikrut rail aarakshan pranali main unki pahchaan kaa koi praavdhaan nahin he, jisase yah pataa chal sake ki unhone kitni tikaton kii booking karai he
 The comments report ko sansad ke chaalu satr main pesh kiya jayega
 In this, agents have been asked to take immediate measures to eliminate multiple user ids so that they do not disturb the booking process
 artiese or website agenton kii gatividhiyon par kadi nigaah rakhane ke liye digitalykrut idi kii vyavhaaryata kaa pataa lagane ko kaha gaya he
 Apart from this, the committee has also suggested that the activities of RTSA and website agents should be investigated on a regular basis and that only those RTSA licenses should be renewed
